After a lot emails, he said he would only give me 300.  A few auto body guys stepped in and said the fenders need a ton of work and that 300 was to low but I  still said fine, its going to cost me more to ship them back. I took a screen shot of his response and conditions. He is going to say he offered a return label, but that wasn't until he got drug on facebook for trying to pass off bad fenders. We had agreed that I would take the fenders down if he paid for the fender repairs and we both would move on. Well he backed out and canceled the electric check he sent me.  He claims extortion, threatens to sue people for defamation who don't agree with him and then blocks them. He will do anything to save his skin. Just watch what he responds with. It got so bad at one point, the owner of L5 motorsports (the vendor) reached out to me to try and help. She agreed to help with getting the fenders fixed, but Mike said no . I originally asked for 565.50, as a lot of autobody professionals said that should cover the repairs of the  fenders to make them right. I reached out to Sue and Mike and told that the repairs came in at 485 and that I dont need the full 565.50 I had originally asked for. Sure sounds like I was an extortionist! Mike wanted me to word a post a certain way on Facebook to make me look bad and he the victim. You can see by the responses to negative feedback that its always excuses and never his fault. He is just mad he couldn't buy me off like others. I don't need money. He asked for a review so he gets one. I'm not keeping hush money so that he can hurt others in our great car community.

Oh, hes going to make up lies about how I asked for 57 percent. My original asking price was 562.50, which is 25 percent of my 2200 order for 4 bad fenders. 57 percent of 2200 is 1,254. 1,254 is not 565.50. He also fails to mention the part that after the parts were fixed, I asked for a reimbursement of 485, not the 562.50 he agreed to and then backed out of. So not only is he liar, he cant even do math correctly.

You have to ask yourself if you are comfortable doing business with a company that offers hush money.

< Text>
Talked to Mike about getting my manual transmission swapped on my 2011 Mustang, and everyone who knows, knows the MT-82 in this thing is made out of glass. I located a transmission that came out of a 2014.

Some concerns were raised about my car after I poked around on the forums, such as the clutch may not fit the flywheel because some of the first run 2011's had 2010 flywheels. Mike researched all the parts, and found a clutch that would work for both, got all the parts in before I dropped off the car.

Ed who is the head tech, is very knowledgeable and really kept me in the loop every step of the way. We ran into an issue where a solenoid was no longer present on the newer versions of the transmissions. Because this version was only in use for 2 it was very specific. Ed called me, told me the trouble, we talked it out, and he said he'll do some research and come up a solution. 30 minutes later he came through with a workaround, and we were all set.

They installed a clutch, everything for the replacement transmission, aftermarket short throw shifter and flushed the brake system for me. Upon picking up the car, Ed went over everything with me, and went over break in procedures for the clutch and anything that would need time to adjust.

I will be bringing my cars there for all my future mods that I can't wrench myself.

The TLDR version:

My car's transmissions is trash, Mike found parts that I needed for a swap, Ed the lead tech worked on the car and did a great job. Every issue we ran into, TPS came up with a solution. You should not hesitate to bring your car to them.</Text>

< review>
My experience with this company was an excellent one.  My new corvette broke down late at night and I called another towing place who promised me they'd be there in 30 minutes.  About 30 minutes later, they called me back to tell me that it would be another 2 hours, minimum.  I called another place and they simply didn't pick up the phone.  The 3rd place I called was College Oak Towing.  They told me they'd be there in 30-45 minutes and managed to get there in 20 minutes.  The driver, Jerry, was very capable and gentle with my expensive car.  To those of you unfamiliar with towing, it's not easy to avoid scraping a car that rides as low as mine.  He used wood blocks and careful manipulation of the wheels and my brake input, and as a result my car was successfully towed to my house without any issues, and without a single bump or scrape.  In addition to all of this, the dispatcher that I dealt with was very polite and understanding of my situation.  This was unlike the other company I'd called, who seemed impatient and didn't walk me through the process very nicely.  As a business owner myself, I pay very close attention to the customer service of companies, particular those companies whose services don't really obligate them to be nice to you.  Other towing companies should learn from the example of this one.  I would definitely call College Oak Towing first in the future, as I honestly wouldn't trust anyone else with my car, or with my time.</review>

<Rating>4</Rating><review>This pho place was a lot nicer and cleaner than most I've been to. The restaurant was decently sized and there was even a bar. I used a yelp deal and got Cajun garlic truffle fries with my pho tai (rare steak). There were so many different flavored fries! I love that these fries were thin and crispy. The ones I got were kind of spicy but there were other flavors you could have gotten too! I chose the Cajun garlic truffle because they were literally all the flavors I love on my fries and I've NEVER seen fries with all three seasonings!! I would come back just for the fries. You could just order the fries for $3 also.

I was hungry so I got the pho. The meat was pretty tough but I'm not sure if it was just my pho or if it's normally like that. I honestly think the fries are better than the pho... but I have a bias towards fries as you can tell. Overall, I would come here again to eat<//review>< pics>

If there's an office party, I shop for the pastries. The blackberry & raspberry are popular at the office parties I attended. Moreover, also, the freshly prepared pizza is really worthwhile!

Spoiled as I remember how Whole Foods use to be. Now even the food bar closes early, was 9;30, then 9:15, now back to 8:30, and now stocked with broad selection of fattier heavy carb foods. < review>
Like any Whole Foods this is on the high end of grocery stores in terms of prices. They have more exotic and organic ingredients. The quality is generally good and there is a massive selection of almost everything. The store itself has a rather chaotic layout. Its difficult to find what you need unless you've been there before and its usually quite crowded. That said if you just need something very specific and you don't paying a little more its a good place to grocery shop. Surprisingly they have a fairly decent craft beer selection as well.</review>
